if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_7();
	if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') != 'a5b21a9b8bd4095e35afb0912d873ff5b42ee98c') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'a5b21a9b8bd4095e35afb0912d873ff5b42ee98c') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'c5de6ea5e35fa407409afad8757a3d6ed4b8736a') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'a5b21a9b8bd4095e35afb0912d873ff5b42ee98c') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}

	if (@sha1_file('plugins/sqlSlang/sqlite/OIDplusSqlSlangPluginSQLite.class.php') !== '44da6e1b5e142e9563636341569c9601ca7a67b8') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/sqlSlang/sqlite/OIDplusSqlSlangPluginSQLite.class.php') !== '9156cf955e7b039517e5af5f0f8d427e005bca83') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/sqlSlang/sqlite/OIDplusSqlSlangPluginSQLite.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/sqlSlang/sqlite/OIDplusSqlSlangPluginSQLite.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/sqlSlang/sqlite/OIDplusSqlSlangPluginSQLite.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/sqlSlang/sqlite/OIDplusSqlSlangPluginSQLite.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_16();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/sqlSlang/sqlite/OIDplusSqlSlangPluginSQLite.class.php') !== '44da6e1b5e142e9563636341569c9601ca7a67b8') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/sqlSlang/sqlite/OIDplusSqlSlangPluginSQLite.class.php');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 433\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 433') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
